FNV LOD HANDOFF AND SCHEDULER FOLLOW-UP AUDIT

This follow-up closes gaps left by the two broad LOD audits:
1. Exact IOManager and IOTask virtual-slot ownership from submission through worker execution and completion.
2. Exact AttachDistant3DTask submission, cancellation, and main-thread real-3D publication path.
3. Exact TESObjectCELL +0xA8 total and +0xAA ready counter lifecycle, retirement guard, and retirement action.
4. Raw bodies for undefined NiLOD and BSFade virtual targets that can affect selection, traversal, or visibility.
